   451	        /// <summary>

   455	
   456	        #region Life cycle management
   457	
   458	        /// <inheritdoc />
   459	        public MudTabs()
   460	        {
   461	            _panels = new List<MudTabPanel>();
   462	            Panels = _panels.AsReadOnly();
   463	            _throttleDispatcher = new Lazy<ThrottleDispatcher>(() => new ThrottleDispatcher(500, TimeProvider));
   464	            using var registerScope = CreateRegisterScope();
   465	            _activePanelIndexState = registerScope.RegisterParameter<int>(nameof(ActivePanelIndex))
   466	                .WithParameter(() => ActivePanelIndex)
   467	                .WithEventCallback(() => ActivePanelIndexChanged)
   468	                .WithChangeHandler(HandleActivePanelIndexChanged);
   469	        }
   470	
   471	        /// <inheritdoc />
   472	        protected override void OnInitialized()
   473	        {
   474	            _resizeObserver = _resizeObserverFactory.Create();
   475	            _tabListId = $"tablist-{_componentId}";
   476	            base.OnInitialized();
   477	        }
   478	
   479	        /// <inheritdoc />
   480	        protected override void OnParametersSet()
   481	        {
   482	            base.OnParametersSet();
   483	
   484	            _resizeObserver ??= _resizeObserverFactory.Create();
   485	
   486	            _nextIcon = RightToLeft ? PrevIcon : NextIcon;
   487	            _prevIcon = RightToLeft ? NextIcon : PrevIcon;
   488	            _isVerticalTabs = Position is Position.Left or Position.Right or Position.Start or Position.End;
   489	        }
   490	
   491	        /// <inheritdoc />
   492	        public override async Task SetParametersAsync(ParameterView parameters)
   493	        {
   494	            var dragAndDropChanged = parameters.TryGetValue<bool>(nameof(EnableDragAndDrop), out var _);
   495	            var positionChanged = parameters.TryGetValue<Position>(nameof(Position), out var _);
   496	            if (dragAndDropChanged || positionChanged)
   497	            {
   498	                // need to recalculate the layout since drag and drop and position
   499	                // changes the tab structure more broadly
   500	                _redraw = true;
   501	                _isVerticalTabs = Position is Position.Left or Position.Right or Position.Start or Position.End;
   502	            }
   503	            await base.SetParametersAsync(parameters);
   504	        }
   505	
   506	        /// <inheritdoc />
   507	        protected override async Task OnAfterRenderAsync(bool firstRender)
   508	        {
   509	            await base.OnAfterRenderAsync(firstRender);
   510	
   511	            if (firstRender)
   512	            {
   513	                // add observer to inner and outer tab container to detect size changes
   514	                // specifically for when the browser is resized, we need the inner 
   515	                // observed since the content is width: 100% it'll bubble size changes to parent
   516	                var items = new HashSet<ElementReference>(ResizeObserver.ElementReferenceComparer.Default)
   517	                {
   518	                    _tabsInnerSize,
   519	                    _tabsContentSize
   520	                };
   521	
   522	                await _resizeObserver!.Observe(items);
   523	
   524	                _resizeObserver.OnResized += OnResized;
   525	
   526	                // fix ActivePanelIndex on initial render
   527	                // https://github.com/MudBlazor/MudBlazor/issues/11519
   528	                // must have an active panel to set scroll states                
   529	
   530	                var startingIndex = _activePanelIndexState.Value;
   531	                var index = FindNearestValidPanelIndex(startingIndex);
   532	
   533	                if (index.HasValue && index.Value != startingIndex)
   534	                {
   535	                    // update the ActivePanelIndex to be valid
   536	                    await _activePanelIndexState.SetValueAsync(index.Value);
   537	                }
   538	
   539	                var options = new KeyInterceptorOptions(
   540	                    "mud-tab",
   541	                    [
   542	                        // prevent scrolling page
   543	                        new(" ", preventDown: "key+none", preventUp: "key+none"),
   544	                        new("Enter", preventDown: "key+none"),
   545	                        new("NumpadEnter", preventDown: "key+none"),
   546	                        new("Backspace", preventDown: "key+none")
   547	                    ]);
   548	
   549	                await KeyInterceptorService.SubscribeAsync(_elementId, options, keyDown: HandleKeyInterceptorAsync);
   550	                _redraw = true;
   551	                await InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
   552	            }
   553	            else if (_redraw)
   554	            {
   555	                _redraw = false;
   556	                await CalculateLayoutAsync();
   557	                await UpdateVisualStateAsync();
   558	            }
   559	        }
   560	
   561	        /// <summary>
   562	        /// Called to dispose this instance.
   563	        /// </summary>
   564	        protected virtual async ValueTask DisposeAsyncCore()
   565	        {
   566	            if (_isDisposed)
   567	            {
   568	                return;
   569	            }
   570	
   571	            _isDisposed = true;
   572	
   573	            if (_throttleDispatcher.IsValueCreated)
   574	            {
   575	                _throttleDispatcher.Value.Dispose();
   576	            }
   577	
   578	            if (_resizeObserver is not null)
   579	            {
   580	                _resizeObserver.OnResized -= OnResized;
   581	                if (IsJSRuntimeAvailable)
   582	                {
   583	                    await _resizeObserver.DisposeAsync();
   584	                }
   585	            }
   586	
   587	            if (IsJSRuntimeAvailable)
   588	            {
   589	                await KeyInterceptorService.UnsubscribeAsync(_elementId);
   590	            }
   591	        }
   592	
   593	        /// <summary>
   594	        /// Releases resources used by this component.
   595	        /// </summary>
   596	        public async ValueTask DisposeAsync()
   597	        {
   598	            await DisposeAsyncCore();
   599	            GC.SuppressFinalize(this);
   600	        }
   601	
   602	        #endregion
   603	
   604	        #region Children
   605	
   606	        internal async Task AddPanelAsync(MudTabPanel tabPanel)
   607	        {
   608	            _panels.Add(tabPanel);
   609	            SortPanels();
   610	
   611	            var activeIndex = _activePanelIndexState.Value;
   612	            var activePanel = ActivePanel;
   613	
   614	            if (activeIndex == -1)
   615	            {
   616	                // if no index set
   617	                await _activePanelIndexState.SetValueAsync(_panels.IndexOf(tabPanel));
   618	            }
   619	            else if (activePanel != null && activeIndex != _panels.IndexOf(activePanel))
   620	            {
   621	                // if sortpanels changed the index readjust
   622	                await _activePanelIndexState.SetValueAsync(_panels.IndexOf(activePanel));
   623	            }
   624	            _redraw = true;
   625	            await InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
   626	        }
   627	
   628	        internal async Task SetPanelRefAsync(ElementReference reference)
   629	        {
   630	            if (HasRendered && _resizeObserver!.IsElementObserved(reference) == false)
   631	                await _resizeObserver!.Observe(reference);
   632	
   633	            _redraw = true;
   634	            await InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
   635	        }
   636	
   637	        internal async Task RemovePanel(MudTabPanel tabPanel)
   638	        {
   639	            if (_isDisposed)
   640	                return;
   641	
   642	            await _resizeObserver!.Unobserve(tabPanel.PanelRef);
   643	
   644	            var index = _panels.IndexOf(tabPanel);
   645	            var wasActive = _activePanelIndexState.Value == index;
   646	            var activePanel = ActivePanel;
   647	
   648	            _panels.RemoveAt(index);
   649	
   650	            // no panels left that are visible and not disabled
   651	            if (!_panels.Any(x => x.Visible && !x.Disabled))
   652	            {
   653	                await _activePanelIndexState.SetValueAsync(-1);
   654	            }
   655	            else if (wasActive) // if removed tab was active, choose a new one
   656	            {
   657	                // either the last panel or the panel in the existing index whichever is lower
   658	                var newIndex = FindNearestValidPanelIndex(index);
   659	                if (!newIndex.HasValue)
   660	                    await _activePanelIndexState.SetValueAsync(-1);
   661	                else
   662	                    await _activePanelIndexState.SetValueAsync(newIndex.Value);
   663	            }
   664	            else if (activePanel != null) // update index
   665	            {
   666	                await _activePanelIndexState.SetValueAsync(_panels.IndexOf(activePanel));
   667	            }
   668	            // queue a redraw if needed
   669	            if (!_redraw)
   670	            {
   671	                _redraw = true;
   672	                await InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
   673	            }
   674	        }
   675	
   676	        /// <summary>
   677	        /// Finds the nearest valid panel index that is Visible and not Disabled.
   678	        /// Preference is given to panels to the left (previous tabs).
   679	        /// </summary>
   680	        private int? FindNearestValidPanelIndex(int startIndex)
   681	        {
   682	            if (!_panels.Any())
   683	            {
   684	                // nothing to find if no panels
   685	                return null;
   686	            }
   687	            // Clamp starting point
   688	            startIndex = Math.Clamp(startIndex, 0, _panels.Count - 1);
   689	            // If the provided index is good stop here.
   690	            if (_panels[startIndex] is { Visible: true, Disabled: false })
   691	                return startIndex;
   692	
   693	            // Search to the left
   694	            for (int i = startIndex; i >= 0; i--)
   695	            {
   696	                if (_panels[i].Visible && !_panels[i].Disabled)
   697	                    return i;
   698	            }
   699	            // Search to the right
   700	            for (int i = startIndex + 1; i < _panels.Count; i++)
   701	            {
   702	                if (_panels[i].Visible && !_panels[i].Disabled)
   703	                    return i;
   704	            }
   705	            return null;
   706	        }
   707	
   708	        /// <summary>
   709	        /// Handles when ActivePanelIndex is changed outside of the component
   710	        /// </summary>
   711	        private Task HandleActivePanelIndexChanged(ParameterChangedEventArgs<int> args)
   712	        {
   713	            return ActivatePanelAsync(args.Value);
   714	        }
   715	
   716	        /// <summary>
   717	        /// Sets the active panel and <see cref="ActivePanelIndex"/> property to match the provided index. 
   718	        /// An invalid index is discarded and no changes are made.
   719	        /// </summary>
   720	        /// <param name="index">The index of the panel to activate.</param>
   721	        /// <param name="ignoreDisabledState">When <c>true</c>, the panel will be activated even if it is disabled.</param>
   722	        public Task ActivatePanelAsync(int index, bool ignoreDisabledState = false)
   723	        {
   724	            if (index < 0 || index >= _panels.Count)
   725	                return Task.CompletedTask;
   726	
   727	            return ActivatePanelAsync(_panels[index], ignoreDisabledState);
   728	        }
   729	
   730	        /// <summary>
   731	        /// Sets the active panel and <see cref="ActivePanelIndex"/> property to match the provided unique id. 
   732	        /// An invalid id is discarded and no changes are made.
   733	        /// </summary>
   734	        /// <param name="id">The unique ID of the panel to activate.</param>
   735	        /// <param name="ignoreDisabledState">When <c>true</c>, the panel will be activated even if it is disabled.</param>
   736	        public Task ActivatePanelAsync(object id, bool ignoreDisabledState = false)
   737	        {
   738	            var panel = _panels.FirstOrDefault(p => Equals(p.ID, id));
   739	            return panel is null
   740	                ? Task.CompletedTask
   741	                : ActivatePanelAsync(panel, ignoreDisabledState);
   742	        }
   743	
   744	        /// <summary>
   745	        /// Sets the active panel and <see cref="ActivePanelIndex"/> property to match the provided panel. 
   746	        /// A <c>null</c> panel deactivates all panels.
   747	        /// </summary>
   748	        /// <param name="panel">The panel to activate. <c>null</c> to deactivate.</param>
   749	        /// <param name="ignoreDisabledState">When <c>true</c>, the panel will be activated even if it is disabled.</param>
   750	        public async Task ActivatePanelAsync(MudTabPanel? panel, bool ignoreDisabledState = false)
   751	        {
   752	            if (panel == null)
   753	            {
   754	                await _activePanelIndexState.SetValueAsync(-1);
   755	            }
   756	            else if (panel.Visible && (!panel.Disabled || ignoreDisabledState))
   757	            {
   758	                var index = _panels.IndexOf(panel);
   759	                var previewArgs = new TabInteractionEventArgs
   760	                {
   761	                    PanelIndex = index,
   762	                    InteractionType = TabInteractionType.Activate
   763	                };
   764	
   765	                if (OnPreviewInteraction != null)
   766	                    await OnPreviewInteraction.Invoke(previewArgs);
   767	
   768	                if (previewArgs.Cancel) return;
   769	
   770	                await _activePanelIndexState.SetValueAsync(previewArgs.PanelIndex);
   771	            }
   772	            _redraw = true;
   773	            await InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
   774	        }
   775	
   776	        private async Task ActivatePanelClickAsync(MudTabPanel panel, MouseEventArgs ev, bool ignoreDisabledState = false)
   777	        {
   778	            await ActivatePanelAsync(panel, ignoreDisabledState);
   779	            await panel.OnClick.InvokeAsync(ev);
   780	        }
   781	
   782	        private void SortPanels()
   783	        {
   784	            if (_panels.Count == 0 || (SortDirection == SortDirection.None && SortComparer is null))
   785	                return;
   786	
   787	            _panels.Sort(GetTabSortExpression);
   788	        }
   789	
   790	        private int GetTabSortExpression(MudTabPanel a, MudTabPanel b)
   791	        {
   792	            if (SortComparer is not null)
   793	            {
   794	                return SortComparer.Compare(a, b);
   795	            }
   796	
   797	            var dir = SortDirection is SortDirection.Ascending ? 1 : -1;
   798	            return Comparer.Default.Compare(GetTabSortKey(a), GetTabSortKey(b)) * dir;
   799	        }
   800	
   801	        private static string? GetTabSortKey(MudTabPanel panel) => panel.SortKey ?? panel.Text;
   802	        #endregion

   835	        /// <summary>

   840	            new StyleBuilder()

   842	                .AddStyle("transform", $"translateY({(-1 * _scrollPosition).ToString(CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)}px)", _isVerticalTabs)

   878	                .AddStyle("transition", SliderAnimation ? "right .3s cubic-bezier(.64,.09,.08,1);" : "none", Position is Position.Top or Position.Bottom)
   879	                .AddStyle("transition", SliderAnimation ? "top .3s cubic-bezier(.64,.09,.08,1);" : "none", _isVerticalTabs)
   880	                .AddStyle("height", _sliderSizePercentage.ToPercent(), _isVerticalTabs)
   881	                .AddStyle("top", _sliderPositionPercentage.ToPercent(), _isVerticalTabs)
   882	                .Build()
   883	            : new StyleBuilder()
   884	                .AddStyle("width", _sliderSizePercentage.ToPercent(), Position is Position.Top or Position.Bottom)
   885	                .AddStyle("left", _sliderPositionPercentage.ToPercent(), Position is Position.Top or Position.Bottom)
   886	                .AddStyle("transition", SliderAnimation ? "left .3s cubic-bezier(.64,.09,.08,1);" : "none", Position is Position.Top or Position.Bottom)
   887	                .AddStyle("transition", SliderAnimation ? "top .3s cubic-bezier(.64,.09,.08,1);" : "none", _isVerticalTabs)
   888	                .AddStyle("height", _sliderSizePercentage.ToPercent(), _isVerticalTabs)
   889	                .AddStyle("top", _sliderPositionPercentage.ToPercent(), _isVerticalTabs)
   890	                .Build();
   891	
   892	        private Position ConvertPosition(Position position)
   893	        {
   894	            return position switch
   895	            {
   896	                Position.Start => RightToLeft ? Position.Right : Position.Left,
   897	                Position.End => RightToLeft ? Position.Left : Position.Right,
   898	                _ => position
   899	            };
   900	        }
   901	
   902	        private string GetTabClass(MudTabPanel panel)
   903	        {
   904	            var tabClass = new CssBuilder("mud-tab")
   905	              .AddClass($"mud-tab-active", when: () => panel == ActivePanel)
   906	              .AddClass($"mud-disabled", panel.Disabled)
   907	              .AddClass($"mud-ripple", Ripple)
   908	              .AddClass(ActiveTabClass, when: () => panel == ActivePanel)
   909	              .AddClass(TabButtonsClass)
   910	              .AddClass(panel.Classname)
   911	              .Build();
   912	
   913	            return tabClass;
   914	        }
   915	
   916	        private Placement GetTooltipPlacement()
   917	        {
   918	            return Position switch
   919	            {
   920	                Position.Right => Placement.Left,
   921	                Position.Left => Placement.Right,
   922	                Position.Bottom => Placement.Top,
   923	                _ => Placement.Bottom
   924	            };
   925	        }
   926	
   927	        private string GetTabStyle(MudTabPanel panel)
   928	        {
   929	            var tabStyle = new StyleBuilder()
   930	                .AddStyle("min-width", MinimumTabWidth)
   931	                .AddStyle(panel.Style)
   932	                .Build();
   933	
   934	            return tabStyle;
   935	        }
   936	
   937	        private Color GetPanelIconColor(MudTabPanel panel)
   938	        {
   939	            if (panel.Disabled)
   940	            {
   941	                return Color.Inherit;
   942	            }
   943	
   944	            if (panel.IconColor != default)
   945	            {
   946	                return panel.IconColor;
   947	            }
   948	
   949	            return IconColor;
   950	        }

   954	        #region Rendering and placement
   955	
   956	        /// <summary>
   957	        /// Calculates the layout sizing of the containers and scroll buttons.
   958	        /// </summary>
   959	        private async Task CalculateLayoutAsync()
   960	        {
   961	            _dropContainer?.Refresh();
   962	            await GetAllReferenceSizes();
   963	            GetAllTabsSize();
   964	            _tabBarContentSize = GetTabBarContentSize();
   965	            SetScrollButtonVisibility();
   966	        }
   967	
   968	        /// <summary>
   969	        /// Determines the visual state of the component after rendering.
   970	        /// </summary>
   971	        /// <remarks>
   972	        /// Used to update scroll position, scrollability states (scrollprevious and scrollnext buttons), 
   973	        /// and slider state.
   974	        /// </remarks>
   975	        private Task UpdateVisualStateAsync()
   976	        {
   977	            CenterScrollPositionAroundSelectedItem();
   978	            SetScrollabilityStates();
   979	            SetSliderState();
   980	            return InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
   981	        }
   982	
   983	        private async void OnResized(IDictionary<ElementReference, BoundingClientRect> changes)
   984	        {
   985	            if (!_redraw)
   986	            {
   987	                _redraw = true;
   988	                await InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
   989	            }
   990	        }
   991	
   992	        private void SetSliderState()
   993	        {
   994	            if (ActivePanel is null)
   995	            {
   996	                return;
   997	            }
   998	            _sliderPositionPercentage = GetLengthOfPanelItems(ActivePanel) / _allTabsSize * 100;
   999	            _sliderSizePercentage = GetPanelLength(ActivePanel) / _allTabsSize * 100;
  1000	            _isSliderPositionDetermined =
  1001	                (_activePanelIndexState.Value > 0 && _sliderPositionPercentage > 0)
  1002	                || IsFirstVisiblePanel(ActivePanel);
  1003	        }
  1004	
  1005	        /// <summary>
  1006	        /// this sets _tabBarContentSize to the total calculated width of the mud-tabs-tabbar-content
  1007	        /// </summary>
  1008	        private double GetTabBarContentSize()
  1009	        {
  1010	            return GetRelevantSize(_tabsContentSize);
  1011	        }
  1012	
  1013	        private async Task GetAllReferenceSizes()
  1014	        {
  1015	            _tabSizes.Clear();
  1016	            var panelRefs = _panels.Select(x => x.PanelRef).ToList();
  1017	            panelRefs.Add(_tabsContentSize);
  1018	            var tasks = panelRefs.Select(async panelRef => (panelRef, rect: await panelRef.MudGetBoundingClientRectAsync())).ToList();
  1019	            var results = await Task.WhenAll(tasks);
  1020	            foreach (var result in results)
  1021	            {
  1022	                _tabSizes.TryAdd(result.panelRef, result.rect);
  1023	            }
  1024	        }
  1025	
  1026	        private void GetAllTabsSize()
  1027	        {
  1028	            double totalTabsSize = 0;
  1029	
  1030	            foreach (var panel in _panels)
  1031	            {
  1032	                totalTabsSize += GetRelevantSize(panel.PanelRef);
  1033	            }
  1034	
  1035	            _allTabsSize = totalTabsSize;
  1036	        }
  1037	
  1038	        private double GetRelevantSize(ElementReference reference)
  1039	        {
  1040	            // _tabSizes get current values using MudGetBoundingClientRectAsync
  1041	            var success = _tabSizes.TryGetValue(reference, out var rect);
  1042	
  1043	            var height = rect?.Height ?? 0.0;
  1044	            var width = rect?.Width ?? 0.0;
  1045	            const double epsilon = 0.01; // handles any odd rounding errors
  1046	
  1047	            if (Math.Abs(height) < epsilon || Math.Abs(width) < epsilon)
  1048	                success = false;
  1049	
  1050	            // fallback to resizeobserver values if null or 0
  1051	            if (!success)
  1052	            {
  1053	                rect = _resizeObserver!.GetSizeInfo(reference);
  1054	                // ensure we don't return a null value
  1055	                height = rect?.Height ?? 0.0;
  1056	                width = rect?.Width ?? 0.0;
  1057	            }
  1058	
  1059	            return _isVerticalTabs ? height : width;
  1060	        }
  1061	
  1062	        /// <summary>
  1063	        /// Returns the width or height of a subset of panel items up to the panel item selected, depending on tab orientation.
  1064	        /// </summary>
  1065	        /// <remarks>
  1066	        /// If inclusive is true, it returns the width or height of the panel item selected as well.
  1067	        /// For horizontal tabs, this is the width; for vertical tabs, this is the height.
  1068	        /// </remarks>
  1069	        private double GetLengthOfPanelItems(MudTabPanel panel, bool inclusive = false)
  1070	        {
  1071	            var value = 0.0;
  1072	            foreach (var item in _panels)
  1073	            {
  1074	                if (item == panel)
  1075	                {
  1076	                    if (inclusive)
  1077	                    {
  1078	                        value += GetRelevantSize(item.PanelRef);
  1079	                    }
  1080	
  1081	                    break;
  1082	                }
  1083	
  1084	                value += GetRelevantSize(item.PanelRef);
  1085	            }
  1086	
  1087	            return value;
  1088	        }
  1089	
  1090	        private double GetPanelLength(MudTabPanel? panel) => panel == null ? 0.0 : GetRelevantSize(panel.PanelRef);
  1091	
  1092	        private bool IsFirstVisiblePanel(MudTabPanel? activePanel)
  1093	        {
  1094	            foreach (var panel in _panels)
  1095	            {
  1096	                if (activePanel == panel)
  1097	                {
  1098	                    return true;
  1099	                }
  1100	
  1101	                if (panel.Visible)
  1102	                {
  1103	                    return false;
  1104	                }
  1105	            }
  1106	
  1107	            return true;
  1108	        }
  1109	
  1110	        #endregion
  1111	
  1112	        #region scrolling
  1113	
  1114	        /// <summary>
  1115	        /// Sets the visibility of scroll buttons based on the total size of all tabs and the tab bar content size.
  1116	        /// Scroll buttons are shown if AlwaysShowScrollButtons is true or if the tabs exceed the available space.
  1117	        /// </summary>
  1118	        private void SetScrollButtonVisibility()
  1119	        {
  1120	            _showScrollButtons = AlwaysShowScrollButtons || (int)_allTabsSize > (int)_tabBarContentSize;
  1121	        }
  1122	
  1123	        private void ScrollPrev()
  1124	        {
  1125	            if (_panels.Count == 0)
  1126	                return;
  1127	
  1128	            ScrollBy(isNext: false);
  1129	            SetScrollButtonVisibility();
  1130	            SetScrollabilityStates();
  1131	        }
  1132	
  1133	        private void ScrollNext()
  1134	        {
  1135	            ScrollBy(isNext: true);
  1136	            SetScrollabilityStates();
  1137	        }
  1138	
  1139	        /// <summary>
  1140	        /// Scrolls a <see cref="MudTabPanel" /> to the center of the tab content viewport. Will not scroll beyond the bounds of tabs.
  1141	        /// </summary>
  1142	        private void ScrollToItem(MudTabPanel panel, bool isLast = false)
  1143	        {
  1144	            // set start and max scroll
  1145	            double position;
  1146	            // all panels before selected panel
  1147	            var preSize = GetLengthOfPanelItems(panel, false);
  1148	            var panelSize = GetPanelLength(panel);
  1149	            var maxScroll = _allTabsSize - _tabBarContentSize;
  1150	            if (isLast)
  1151	            {
  1152	                // scroll so the right edge of the last tab is flush to the right edge of the mud-tabs-content (visible tab area)
  1153	                position = maxScroll;
  1154	            }
  1155	            else
  1156	            {
  1157	                // normal scroll to center the active tab
  1158	                var viewportCenter = _tabBarContentSize / 2;
  1159	                var panelCenter = panelSize / 2;
  1160	                position = preSize - viewportCenter + panelCenter;
  1161	            }
  1162	            // ensure no extra space past the start or end
  1163	            position = ScrollEdgeAdjust(position, panelSize);
  1164	            // right to left uses negative positioning but only when it's horizontal tabs
  1165	            position = RightToLeft && !_isVerticalTabs ? -position : position;
  1166	            _scrollPosition = position;
  1167	        }
  1168	
  1169	        /// <summary>
  1170	        /// Sets the minimum and maximum scroll position values and clamps scrollposition to it.
  1171	        /// </summary>
  1172	        private double ScrollEdgeAdjust(double position, double panelSize)
  1173	        {
  1174	            var minScroll = 0.0;
  1175	            var maxScroll = Math.Max(0, _allTabsSize - _tabBarContentSize);
  1176	            if (_tabBarContentSize < panelSize)
  1177	            {
  1178	                var tooSmallSize = _tabBarContentSize;
  1179	                maxScroll = Math.Max(0, maxScroll - tooSmallSize);
  1180	                minScroll = Math.Min(maxScroll, tooSmallSize / 2);
  1181	            }
  1182	            return Math.Clamp(position, minScroll, maxScroll);
  1183	        }
  1184	
  1185	        /// <summary>
  1186	        /// Scroll by page; isNext is true to scroll forward (right or down), false to scroll backward (left or up), depending on tab orientation.
  1187	        /// </summary>
  1188	        private void ScrollBy(bool isNext)
  1189	        {
  1190	            if (_panels.Count == 0)
  1191	                return;
  1192	
  1193	            var panel = isNext ? _panels[^1] : _panels[0];
  1194	            var panelSize = GetPanelLength(panel);
  1195	            var scrollAmount = Math.Max(_tabBarContentSize, panelSize); // minimum 1 tab scroll
  1196	            if (!isNext)
  1197	            {
  1198	                scrollAmount = -scrollAmount;
  1199	            }
  1200	            var position = ScrollEdgeAdjust(_scrollPosition + scrollAmount, panelSize);
  1201	            _scrollPosition = position;
  1202	        }
  1203	
  1204	        private void CenterScrollPositionAroundSelectedItem()
  1205	        {
  1206	            var activeIndex = _activePanelIndexState.Value;
  1207	            if (activeIndex < 0)
  1208	                return;
  1209	            if (activeIndex + 1 == _panels.Count)
  1210	            {
  1211	                var lastPanel = _panels.Last();
  1212	                ScrollToItem(lastPanel, true);
  1213	                return;
  1214	            }
  1215	
  1216	            // scroll to the panel
  1217	            ScrollToItem(ActivePanel!);
  1218	        }
  1219	
  1220	        private void SetScrollabilityStates()
  1221	        {
  1222	            var isEnoughSpace = _allTabsSize <= _tabBarContentSize;
  1223	
  1224	            if (isEnoughSpace)
  1225	            {
  1226	                _nextButtonDisabled = true;
  1227	                _prevButtonDisabled = Math.Abs(_scrollPosition) < 0.01;
  1228	            }
  1229	            else
  1230	            {
  1231	                // Disable next button if the last panel is completely visible
  1232	                _nextButtonDisabled = Math.Abs(_scrollPosition) >= GetLengthOfPanelItems(_panels[^1], true) - _tabBarContentSize;
  1233	                _prevButtonDisabled = Math.Abs(_scrollPosition) < 0.01;
  1234	            }
  1235	        }
  1236	
  1237	        #endregion
  1238	
  1239	        internal async Task ItemUpdated(MudItemDropInfo<MudTabPanel> dropItem)
  1240	        {
  1241	            if (dropItem.Item is null)
  1242	            {
  1243	                return;
  1244	            }
  1245	
  1246	            // get the old index where this item was at
  1247	            var oldIndex = _panels.IndexOf(dropItem.Item);
  1248	            // get the new index in _panels using IndexInZone
  1249	            var newIndex = dropItem.IndexInZone;
  1250	
  1251	            // remove the item from the old index
  1252	            _panels.RemoveAt(oldIndex);
  1253	
  1254	            // insert the item at the new index
  1255	            if (newIndex < _panels.Count)
  1256	            {
  1257	                _panels.Insert(newIndex, dropItem.Item);
  1258	            }
  1259	            else
  1260	            {
  1261	                _panels.Add(dropItem.Item);
  1262	            }
  1263	
  1264	            // Set the dragged tab as active
  1265	            await ActivatePanelAsync(dropItem.Item);
  1266	
  1267	            if (OnItemDropped.HasDelegate)
  1268	            {
  1269	                await OnItemDropped.InvokeAsync(dropItem);
  1270	            }
  1271	        }
  1272	
  1273	        /// <summary>
  1274	        /// Handles keyboard navigation for tabs according to W3C accessibility guidelines
  1275	        /// Supports Enter/Space for activation and arrow keys for navigation
  1276	        /// </summary>
  1277	        protected virtual async Task HandleTabKeyDownAsync(KeyboardEventArgs e, MudTabPanel panel)
  1278	        {
  1279	            switch (e.Key)
  1280	            {
  1281	                case "Enter":
  1282	                case " ":
  1283	                    // considered a click
  1284	                    var args = new MouseEventArgs() { Type = e.Key, Detail = 1, ClientX = 0, ClientY = 0 };
  1285	                    await ActivatePanelClickAsync(panel, args);
  1286	                    break;
  1287	
  1288	                case "ArrowLeft":
  1289	                    if (!_isVerticalTabs)
  1290	                    {
  1291	                        await MoveFocusToPreviousTab(panel);
  1292	                    }
  1293	                    break;
  1294	
  1295	                case "ArrowRight":
  1296	                    if (!_isVerticalTabs)
  1297	                    {
  1298	                        await MoveFocusToNextTab(panel);
  1299	                    }
  1300	                    break;
  1301	
  1302	                case "ArrowUp":
  1303	                    if (_isVerticalTabs)
  1304	                    {
  1305	                        await MoveFocusToPreviousTab(panel);
  1306	                    }
  1307	                    break;
  1308	
  1309	                case "ArrowDown":
  1310	                    if (_isVerticalTabs)
  1311	                    {
  1312	                        await MoveFocusToNextTab(panel);
  1313	                    }
  1314	                    break;
  1315	            }
  1316	        }
  1317	
  1318	        private async Task HandleKeyInterceptorAsync(KeyboardEventArgs e)
  1319	        {
  1320	            var focusedPanel = ActivePanel;
  1321	            if (focusedPanel != null)
  1322	            {
  1323	                await HandleTabKeyDownAsync(e, focusedPanel);
  1324	            }
  1325	        }
  1326	
  1327	        /// <summary>
  1328	        /// Allows the user to move to the previous tab using key arrow
  1329	        /// </summary>
  1330	        private async Task MoveFocusToPreviousTab(MudTabPanel currentPanel)
  1331	        {
  1332	            var enabledPanels = _panels.Where(p => !p.Disabled).ToList();
  1333	            if (enabledPanels.Count <= 1) return;
  1334	
  1335	            var currentIndex = enabledPanels.IndexOf(currentPanel);
  1336	            var previousIndex = currentIndex <= 0 ? enabledPanels.Count - 1 : currentIndex - 1;
  1337	            var previousPanel = enabledPanels[previousIndex];
  1338	
  1339	            await FocusPanel(previousPanel);
  1340	        }
  1341	
  1342	        /// <summary>
  1343	        /// Allows the user to move to the next tab using KeyArrow
  1344	        /// </summary>
  1345	        private async Task MoveFocusToNextTab(MudTabPanel currentPanel)
  1346	        {
  1347	            var enabledPanels = _panels.Where(p => !p.Disabled).ToList();
  1348	            if (enabledPanels.Count <= 1) return;
  1349	
  1350	            var currentIndex = enabledPanels.IndexOf(currentPanel);
  1351	            var nextIndex = currentIndex >= enabledPanels.Count - 1 ? 0 : currentIndex + 1;
  1352	            var nextPanel = enabledPanels[nextIndex];
  1353	
  1354	            await FocusPanel(nextPanel);
  1355	        }
  1356	
  1357	        /// <summary>
  1358	        /// Focuses user onto selected panel
  1359	        /// </summary>
  1360	        private static async Task FocusPanel(MudTabPanel panel)
  1361	        {
  1362	            if (panel.PanelRef.Context != null)
  1363	            {
  1364	                await panel.PanelRef.FocusAsync();
  1365	            }
  1366	        }
  1367	
  1368	        /// <summary>
  1369	        /// Generates a unique ID for a tab element using the tab panels field id.
  1370	        /// Required for aria-controls attribute to link tab to its panel.
  1371	        /// </summary>
  1372	        internal string GetTabId(MudTabPanel panel)
  1373	        {
  1374	            return $"tablist-{_componentId}-tab-{panel.FieldId}";
  1375	        }
  1376	
  1377	        /// <summary>
  1378	        /// Generates a unique ID for a tab panel element using the tab panels field id.
  1379	        /// Required for aria-controls attribute to link tab panel to its tab.
  1380	        /// </summary>
  1381	        internal string GetTabPanelId(MudTabPanel panel)
  1382	        {
  1383	            return $"tablist-{_componentId}-tabpanel-{panel.FieldId}";
  1384	        }
  1385	
  1386	        /// <summary>
  1387	        /// Generates a unique ID for a tab list. 
  1388	        /// Required for aria-controls attribute to identify each tablist.
  1389	        /// </summary>
  1390	        internal string GetTabListId()
  1391	        {
  1392	            return _tabListId!;
  1393	        }
  1394	
  1395	        /// <summary>
  1396	        /// Generates a string with the relevant aria label information.
  1397	        /// </summary>
  1398	        internal string GetPrevAriaLabel()
  1399	        {
  1400	            if (_isVerticalTabs)
  1401	                return Localizer[LanguageResource.MudTabs_ScrollUp];
  1402	
  1403	            return RightToLeft
  1404	                ? Localizer[LanguageResource.MudTabs_ScrollRight]
  1405	                : Localizer[LanguageResource.MudTabs_ScrollLeft];
  1406	        }
  1407	
  1408	        /// <summary>
  1409	        /// Generates a string with the relevant aria label information.
  1410	        /// </summary>
  1411	        internal string GetNextAriaLabel()
  1412	        {
  1413	            if (_isVerticalTabs)
  1414	                return Localizer[LanguageResource.MudTabs_ScrollDown];
  1415	
  1416	            return RightToLeft
  1417	                ? Localizer[LanguageResource.MudTabs_ScrollLeft]
  1418	                : Localizer[LanguageResource.MudTabs_ScrollRight];
  1419	        }
  1420	    }
  1421	}

    84	    private RenderFragment RenderTabWrapperSection(MudTabPanel panel) =>
    85	        @<text>
    86	            @if (panel.TabContent is null && panel.TabWrapperContent is null)
    87	            {
    88	                <MudTooltip Placement="@GetTooltipPlacement()" Text="@panel.ToolTip" @key="@panel">
    89	                    @RenderTab(panel)
    90	                </MudTooltip>
    91	            }
    92	            else
    93	            {
    94	                <div class="d-inline-block" style="width: fit-content;" @key="@panel">
    95	                    @if (panel.TabWrapperContent is null)
    96	                    {
    97	                        @RenderTab(panel)
    98	                    }
    99	                    else
   100	                    {
   101	                        @panel.TabWrapperContent(RenderTab(panel))
   102	                    }
   103	                </div>
   104	            }
   105	        </text>;
   106	
   107	    private RenderFragment RenderTab(MudTabPanel panel) =>

   109	              aria-controls="@GetTabPanelId(panel)" role="tab" id="@GetTabId(panel)" aria-selected="@(panel == ActivePanel ? "true" : "false")"
   110	              tabindex="@(panel == ActivePanel ? "0" : "-1")" @onkeydown="@(e => HandleTabKeyDownAsync(e, panel))">

   120	            }
   121	            else if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(panel.Text) && string.IsNullOrEmpty(panel.Icon))
   122	            {
   123	                @panel.Text
   124	            }
   125	            else if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(panel.Text) && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(panel.Icon))
   126	            {
   127	                <MudIcon Icon="@panel.Icon" Color="@GetPanelIconColor(panel)" />
   128	            }
   129	            else if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(panel.Text) && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(panel.Icon))
   130	            {
   131	                <MudIcon Icon="@panel.Icon" Color="@GetPanelIconColor(panel)" Class="mud-tab-icon-text" />

     6	using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components;
     7	using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components.Web;
     8	using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;
     9	using MudBlazor.Services;
    10	using MudBlazor.UnitTests.TestComponents.Tabs;
    11	using MudBlazor.UnitTests.TestComponents.Tabs.KeepTabsAlive;
    12	using NUnit.Framework;
    13	
    14	namespace MudBlazor.UnitTests.Components
    15	{
    16	    [TestFixture]
    17	    public class TabsTests : BunitTest
    18	    {
    19	        [SetUp]
    20	        public override void Setup()
    21	        {
    22	            base.Setup();
    23	            Context.Services.Add(new ServiceDescriptor(typeof(IResizeObserverFactory), new MockResizeObserverFactory()));
    24	        }
    25	
    26	        [Test]
    27	        public async Task AddingAndRemovingTabPanels()
    28	        {
    29	            var comp = Context.Render<TabsAddingRemovingTabsTest>();
    30	            comp.Find("div.mud-tabs-panels").InnerHtml.Trim().Should().BeEmpty();
    31	            comp.FindAll("div.mud-tab").Should().BeEmpty();
    32	            comp.Instance.Tabs.Panels.Should().NotBeNull().And.BeEmpty();
    33	
    34	            // add a panel
    35	            await comp.FindAll("button")[0].ClickAsync();
    36	            comp.Find("div.mud-tabs-panels").InnerHtml.Trim().Should().NotBeEmpty();
    37	            comp.FindAll("div.mud-tab").Count.Should().Be(1);
    38	            comp.FindAll("p.mud-typography").Count.Should().Be(1);
    39	
    40	            comp.Instance.Tabs.Panels.Should().NotBeNull().And.HaveCount(1);
    41	            comp.FindComponents<MudTabPanel>().First().Instance.Should().Be(comp.Instance.Tabs.Panels[0]);
    42	
    43	            // add another
    44	            await comp.FindAll("button")[0].ClickAsync();
    45	            comp.FindAll("div.mud-tab").Count.Should().Be(2);
    46	
    47	            comp.Instance.Tabs.Panels.Should().NotBeNull().And.HaveCount(2);
    48	            comp.FindComponents<MudTabPanel>().ElementAt(0).Instance.Should().Be(comp.Instance.Tabs.Panels[0]);
    49	            comp.FindComponents<MudTabPanel>().ElementAt(1).Instance.Should().Be(comp.Instance.Tabs.Panels[1]);
    50	
    51	            comp.FindAll("p.mud-typography").Count.Should().Be(1, because: "Only the current tab panel is displayed");
    52	            // we are now on tab 0
    53	            comp.Find("p.mud-typography").TrimmedText().Should().Be("Tab 0");
    54	            // switch to tab1
    55	            await comp.FindAll("div.mud-tab")[1].ClickAsync();
    56	            comp.Find("p.mud-typography").TrimmedText().Should().Be("Tab 1");
    57	            // remove tab1
    58	            await comp.FindAll("button")[1].ClickAsync();
    59	            comp.FindAll("div.mud-tab").Count.Should().Be(1);
    60	            comp.FindAll("p.mud-typography").Count.Should().Be(1);
    61	
    62	            comp.Instance.Tabs.Panels.Should().NotBeNull().And.HaveCount(1);
    63	            comp.FindComponents<MudTabPanel>().ElementAt(0).Instance.Should().Be(comp.Instance.Tabs.Panels[0]);
    64	
    65	            // we should be on tab0 again
    66	            comp.Find("p.mud-typography").TrimmedText().Should().Be("Tab 0");
    67	            // remove another
    68	            await comp.FindAll("button")[1].ClickAsync();
    69	            comp.Find("div.mud-tabs-panels").InnerHtml.Trim().Should().BeEmpty();
    70	            comp.FindAll("div.mud-tab").Should().BeEmpty();
    71	
    72	            comp.Instance.Tabs.Panels.Should().NotBeNull().And.BeEmpty();
    73	        }
    74	
    75	        /// <summary>
    76	        /// When KeepPanelsAlive="true" the panels are not destroyed and recreated on tab-switch. We prove that by using a button click counter on every tab and
    77	        /// a callback that is fired only when OnRenderAsync of the tab panel happens the first time (which outputs a message at the bottom).
    78	        /// </summary>
    79	        [Test]
    80	        public async Task KeepTabsAlive()
    81	        {
    82	            var comp = Context.Render<TabsKeepAliveTest>();
    83	            // all panels should be evident in the markup:
    84	            comp.FindAll("button").Count.Should().Be(3);
    85	            // every panel should be rendered first exactly once throughout the test:
    86	            comp.FindAll("p")[^1].MarkupMatches("<p>Panel 1<br>Panel 2<br>Panel 3<br></p>");
    87	            // only the first panel should be active:
    88	            comp.FindAll("div.mud-tabs-panels > div")[0].GetAttribute("style").Should().Be("display:contents;");
    89	            comp.FindAll("div.mud-tabs-panels > div")[1].GetAttribute("style").Should().Be("display:none;");
    90	            comp.FindAll("div.mud-tabs-panels > div")[2].GetAttribute("style").Should().Be("display:none;");
    91	            // click first button and show button click counters
    92	            await comp.FindAll("button")[0].ClickAsync();
    93	            comp.FindAll("button")[0].TrimmedText().Should().Be("Panel 1=1");
    94	            comp.FindAll("button")[1].TrimmedText().Should().Be("Panel 2=0");
    95	            comp.FindAll("button")[2].TrimmedText().Should().Be("Panel 3=0");
    96	            // switch to the second tab:
    97	            await comp.FindAll("div.mud-tab")[1].ClickAsync();
    98	            // none of the panels should have had a render pass with firstRender==true, so this must be as before:
    99	            comp.FindAll("p")[^1].MarkupMatches("<p>Panel 1<br>Panel 2<br>Panel 3<br></p>");
   100	            // second panel should be displayed

- Parent component has `Disabled` property

    [CascadingParameter(Name = "ParentDisabled")]
    private bool ParentDisabled { get; set; }

    /// The reference to the underlying panel element.

    public string? Icon { get; set; }

    [Parameter]
    [Category(CategoryTypes.Tabs.Behavior)]
    public Color IconColor { get; set; }

    /// </summary>
    /// <remarks>
    /// Defaults to <c>false</c>.
    /// </remarks>
    [Parameter]
    [Category(CategoryTypes.Tabs.Behavior)]
    public bool Disabled { get; set; }

    /// </summary>

   116	                    @TabPanelHeader(panel)

   118	            }

import sys

with open('/testbed/src/MudBlazor/Components/Tabs/MudTabPanel.razor.cs', 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

# Add ParentDisabled cascading parameter after Parent cascading parameter
old_str = """    [CascadingParameter]
    private MudTabs? Parent { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// The reference to the underlying panel element."""

new_str = """    [CascadingParameter]
    private MudTabs? Parent { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// If true, the parent <see cref="MudTabs"/> component has disabled all panels.
    /// </summary>
    [CascadingParameter(Name = "ParentDisabled")]
    private bool ParentDisabled { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// The reference to the underlying panel element."""

if old_str in content:
    content = content.replace(old_str, new_str)
else:
    print("ERROR: Could not find old_str")
    sys.exit(1)

# Add IsDisabled property after Disabled property
old_str2 = """    [Category(CategoryTypes.Tabs.Behavior)]
    public bool Disabled { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// Shows the tab."""

new_str2 = """    [Category(CategoryTypes.Tabs.Behavior)]
    public bool Disabled { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// Gets whether this panel is disabled, either directly or via its parent <see cref="MudTabs"/> component.
    /// </summary>
    internal bool IsDisabled => Disabled || ParentDisabled;

    /// <summary>
    /// Shows the tab."""

if old_str2 in content:
    content = content.replace(old_str2, new_str2)
else:
    print("ERROR: Could not find old_str2")
    sys.exit(1)

with open('/testbed/src/MudBlazor/Components/Tabs/MudTabPanel.razor.cs', 'w') as f:
    f.write(content)

print("Done!")
EOF

2026-05-29 15:19:18,437 - INFO - swea-agent-MudBlazor__MudBlazor-12920 - 💭 THOUGHT
All tests pass. Now let me think about edge cases:

1. **MudDynamicTabs**: Since `MudDynamicTabs` inherits from `MudTabs`, it will automatically get the `Disabled` property. The close buttons and add button are rendered via `Header` and `TabPanelHeader` which are inside the `CascadingValue` for `ParentDisabled`. The close buttons (`MudIconButton`) already inherit from `MudBaseButton` which supports `ParentDisabled`. So when `MudTabs.Disabled = true`, the close buttons will also be disabled. This seems like correct behavior.

2. **Scroll buttons**: They are wrapped in `CascadingValue Value="false" Name="ParentDisabled" IsFixed="true"` which overrides the parent's disabled state. So scroll buttons remain enabled even when the tabs component is disabled. This is correct.

3. **The `PrePanelContent`**: It's inside the `ParentDisabled` cascading value, so any buttons inside it would also be disabled. This seems reasonable.

4. **Backwards compatibility**: The `Disabled` property defaults to `false`, so existing code won't be affected.
